<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:inborst.html>inborst</a> (36001)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Loaned from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_High_German" class="extiw" title="w:Middle High German">Middle High German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="gmh">inbrunst</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">passion</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, but reinterpreted as coming from <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">in</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">in</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:borst.html>borst</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">breast, chest</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:inborst.html>inborst</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:inborst.html>inborsten</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:inborst.html>inborstje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>

***incestueus.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:incestueus.html>incestueus</a> (57176)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed, probably from French or English. Equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">incest</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-eus</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:inco.html>inco</a> (105066)</h1><br></body> 
***incognito.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:incognito.html>incognito</a> (24923)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Italian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Italian language">Italian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="it"><a href = vnd.unilang:incognito.html>incognito</a></i>, from <span class="etylcleanup"><span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">incognitus</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">unknown</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <i class="Latn mention" lang="la"><a href = vnd.unilang:in-.html>in-</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">not</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">cognitus</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">known</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <a href = vnd.unilang:perfect.html>perfect</a> passive participle of <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">cognoscere</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:incognito.html>incognito</a></strong> (<i>not comparable</i>)
</p>
<ol><li>without being known; in disguise; in an assumed character, or under an assumed title.
<ul><li><b>1891</b>, Arthur Conan Doyle, <i>A Scandal In Bohemia</i>:
<dl><dd>"But you can understand," <a href = vnd.unilang:said.html>said</a> our strange visitor, sitting down once more and passing his hand <a href = vnd.unilang:over.html>over</a> his high white forehead, “you can understand that I am not accustomed to doing such business in my own person. Yet the matter <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> so delicate that I could not confide it to an <a href = vnd.unilang:agent.html>agent</a> without putting myself in his power. I have come <b><a href = vnd.unilang:incognito.html>incognito</a></b> from Prague for the purpose of consulting you.”</dd></dl></li></ul></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p>This term <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:said.html>said</a> especially of great <a href = vnd.unilang:personages.html>personages</a> who sometimes adopt a disguise or an assumed character in order to avoid notice.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adverb">Adverb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:incognito.html>incognito</a></strong> (<i>not comparable</i>)
</p>
<ol><li>Without revealing one's identity.</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:incognito.html>incognito</a></strong> (<i>countable and uncountable</i>, <i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">incognitos</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>One unknown or in disguise, or under an assumed character or name.</li>
<li>The assumption of disguise or of a feigned character; the state of being in disguise or not recognized.
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1814</b> July 7,  <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Walter_Scott" class="extiw" title="w:Walter Scott">[<a href = vnd.unilang:walter.html>Walter</a> Scott]</a>,  <cite><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Waverley_(novel)" class="extiw" title="w:Waverley (novel)">Waverley; or, ’<a href = vnd.unilang:tis.html>Tis</a> Sixty Years Since. In Three <a href = vnd.unilang:volumes.html>Volumes</a></a></cite>, volume <span class="maintenance-line" style="color: 777777;">(please specify |volume=I, II, or III)</span>, Edinburgh |  Printed by <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/James_Ballantyne" class="extiw" title="w:James Ballantyne">James Ballantyne and Co.</a> for <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Constable_%26_Robinson" class="extiw" title="w:Constable amp; Robinson">Archibald Constable and Co.</a>; London: <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Longman" class="extiw" title="w:Longman">Longman, <a href = vnd.unilang:hurst.html>Hurst</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:rees.html>Rees</a>, Orme, and Brown</a>, <small><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/OCLC" class="extiw" title="w:OCLC">OCLC</a> <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://worldcat.org/oclc/270129598">270129598</a></small>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">His <b><a href = vnd.unilang:incognito.html>incognito</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> endangered.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li></ol>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zelfstandig_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zelfstandig.html>Zelfstandig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:incognito.html>incognito</a></b> <span style="background-color: f8f9fa;border-radius: 2px;border: 1px solid c8ccd1;padding: 0 0.2em 0 0.1em;font-style: italic"><a href = vnd.unilang:o.html>o</a></span>

<ol><li><a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:verborgen.html>verborgen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:houden.html>houden</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:identiteit.html>identiteit</a></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:incontinent.html>incontinent</a> (75259)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr"><a href = vnd.unilang:incontinent.html>incontinent</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/New_Latin" class="extiw" title="w:New Latin">New Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">incontinens</i>. <p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Late_Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Late Latin">Late Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la"><a href = vnd.unilang:incubus.html>incubus</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">incubo</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">nightmare, one who lies down on the sleeper</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">incubare</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to lie upon, to hatch</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>

***indien.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:indien.html>indien</a> (4491)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">in</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">in</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:die.html>die</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">this</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, with <i><a href = vnd.unilang:die.html>die</a></i> in the now obsolete masculine dative/accusative case.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Conjunction">Conjunction</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:indien.html>indien</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">formal</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> if
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:raadpleeg.html>Raadpleeg</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:uw.html>uw</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:arts.html>arts</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:indien.html>indien</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:u.html>u</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:andere.html>andere</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:geneesmiddel.html>geneesmiddelen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:neemt.html>neemt</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">Consult your physician <b>if</b> you are taking other medicines.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***industrie.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:industrie.html>industrie</a> (8034)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_French" class="extiw" title="w:Middle French">Middle French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="frm"><a href = vnd.unilang:industrie.html>industrie</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">industria</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:industrie.html>industrie</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:industrie.html>industrieën</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:industrie.html>industrietje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>An industry, business(es) that produce(s) goods or services</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">obsolete</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> Diligence, industriousness.</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:fabriek.html>fabriek</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl">fabriekswezen</span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">nijverheid</span></li></ul>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zelfstandig_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zelfstandig.html>Zelfstandig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:industrie.html>industrie</a></b> <span style="background-color: f8f9fa;border-radius: 2px;border: 1px solid c8ccd1;padding: 0 0.2em 0 0.1em;font-style: italic">v</span>
</p>
<ol><li>nijverheid</li></ol>
<hr><h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Afgeleide_begrippen"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:afgeleide.html>Afgeleide</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:begrippen.html>begrippen</a></i></span></h5>

***industrieel.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:industrieel.html>industrieel</a> (19404)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">industriel</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">industria</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">industry, zeal</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:industrieel.html>industrieel</a></strong> (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:industrieel.html>industriëler</a></b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl">industrieelst</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>industrial, concerning an industry or industry in general</li>
<li>Produced by an industry, not artisanally</li></ol>
